UEFA Champions League football returns to City


 
Dear Adam,


 
It's fair to say our season has started ok. A hard-fought home win, followed by a useful point at Liverpool. It's QPR next, without a win so far, and they'll be desperate for three points. A stern test is on the cards, so we'll have to work hard to get the right result.


 
Talking of stern tests, the UEFA Champions League group stage draw took place yesterday. We're in Group D along with Real Madrid, Ajax and Borussia Dortmund. It's safe to say there will be no easy games, but remember, these are the kind of matches we want to be involved in. It's a chance to test ourselves against the best. Bring it on!


QPR 
preview


Liverpool 
highlights


Win 
a signed shirt


What 
we're watching

http://www.mcfc.co.uk/citytv/Match-highlights/2012/August/Liverpool-v-City-extended-highlights 

http://www.mcfc.co.uk 

http://www.mcfc.co.uk/citytv/Match-highlights/2012/August/Liverpool-v-City-extended-highlights 

A point at Anfield is a decent result and could prove valuable come the end of the season. We might have finished with nothing had it not been for the alertness of Yaya Toure and Carlos Tevez. Both players pounced on defensive mistakes to ensure honours finished even. 
 

Next up we welcome back Mark Hughes and his QPR side. They've not had the best results this season, which means they'll have a point to prove. They were certainly no pushover last time we met and we'll need a strong performance if we are to maintain our good start to the season.

    <td valign="top" width="277" height="351" bgcolor="#000001" background="http://image.keymail-email.com/lib/fecd15717d67077f/m/1/17157_10.jpg">

  <tr>
    <td valign="top"><img src="http://image.keymail-email.com/lib/fecd15717d67077f/m/1/spacer.gif" width="20" height="351" border="0" style="display: block;"/></td>
    <td valign="top" align="left" width="237" style="font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size:11px; color:#FFFFFF;">
    <strong>UEFA Champions League football returns to City</strong><br /><br />
   
    Dear Adam,<br /><br />
                               
                It's fair to say our season has started ok. A hard-fought home win, followed by a useful point at Liverpool. It's QPR next, without a win so far, and they'll be desperate for three points. A stern test is on the cards, so we'll have to work hard to get the right result.<br /><br />
               
                Talking of stern tests, the UEFA Champions League group stage draw took place yesterday. We're in Group D along with Real Madrid, Ajax and Borussia Dortmund. It's safe to say there will be no easy games, but remember, these are the kind of matches we want to be involved in. It's a chance to test ourselves against the best. Bring it on!
</td>
    <td valign="top"><img src="http://image.keymail-email.com/lib/fecd15717d67077f/m/1/spacer.gif" width="20" height="351" border="0" style="display: block;"/></td>
